338                     MB\_ICONQUESTION | MB\_YESNOCANCEL | MB\_DEFBUTTON1);
339             pick4u = (box\_result == IDYES) ? \textcolor{charliteral}{'y'} : (box\_result == IDNO) ? \textcolor{charliteral}{'n'} : \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)033'};
340         \textcolor{comment}{/* tty\_putstr(BASE\_WINDOW, 0, prompt); */}
341         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{
342         \textcolor{comment}{/* pick4u = lowc(readchar()); */}
343         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{uudecode_8c_ac82f3cc16110a05458f2b2483236afb7}{index}(\hyperlink{decl_8h_acf3ecfe1055b7bede365ef39613f2b7c}{quitchars}, pick4u)) pick4u = \textcolor{charliteral}{'y'};
344         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(!\hyperlink{uudecode_8c_ac82f3cc16110a05458f2b2483236afb7}{index}(\hyperlink{decl_8h_a435ebb3887b48075c97ff301b972ba1b}{ynqchars}, pick4u));
345         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})strlen(prompt) + 1 < \hyperlink{winext_8h_abdcb66bae1fc240beb333f1932bdc30d}{CO}) \{
346         \textcolor{comment}{/* Echo choice and move back down line */}
347         \textcolor{comment}{/* tty\_putsym(BASE\_WINDOW, (int)strlen(prompt)+1, echoline, pick4u); */}
348         \textcolor{comment}{/* tty\_putstr(BASE\_WINDOW, 0, ""); */}
349         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
350         \textcolor{comment}{/* Otherwise it's hard to tell where to echo, and things are}
351 \textcolor{comment}{         * wrapping a bit messily anyway, so (try to) make sure the next}
352 \textcolor{comment}{         * question shows up well and doesn't get wrapped at the}
353 \textcolor{comment}{         * bottom of the window.}
354 \textcolor{comment}{         */}
355         \textcolor{comment}{/* tty\_clear\_nhwindow(BASE\_WINDOW) */} ;
356         
357         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pick4u != \textcolor{charliteral}{'y'} && pick4u != \textcolor{charliteral}{'n'}) \{
358 give\_up:    \textcolor{comment}{/* Quit */}
359         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (selected) \hyperlink{winproto_8h_a4bbec68d324de17b99fecede64b383ba}{free}((\hyperlink{tradstdc_8h_ad4a7dab7269b4b00e3c7c7d2e66f31cd}{genericptr\_t}) selected);
360         \hyperlink{sys_2wince_2mswproc_8c_aa32bde5286c21c371bf075670d1a85aa}{bail}((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *)0);
361         \textcolor{comment}{/*NOTREACHED*/}
362         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};
363         \}
364     \}
